# IMPORTANT: Source Code Access

**Local source files are not present.** Your workspace does not contain source code. You **MUST** use Sourcegraph MCP tools to discover, read, and understand code before making any changes.

**Target Repositories (version-pinned mirrors):**

- `github.com/sg-evals/kubernetes--v1.32.0` — use `repo:^github.com/sg-evals/kubernetes--v1.32.0$` filter
- `github.com/sg-evals/client-go--v0.32.0` — use `repo:^github.com/sg-evals/client-go--v0.32.0$` filter
- `github.com/sg-evals/api--v0.32.0` — use `repo:^github.com/sg-evals/api--v0.32.0$` filter
- `github.com/sg-evals/etcd-io-etcd` — use `repo:^github.com/sg-evals/etcd-io-etcd$` filter

Scope ALL keyword_search/nls_search queries to these repos.
Use the repo name as the `repo` parameter for read_file/go_to_definition/find_references.


## Required Workflow

1. **Search first** — Use MCP tools to find relevant files and understand existing patterns
2. **Read remotely** — Use `sg_read_file` to read full file contents from Sourcegraph
3. **Edit locally** — Use Edit, Write, and Bash to create or modify files in your working directory
4. **Verify locally** — Run tests with Bash to check your changes

## Tool Selection

| Goal | Tool |
|------|------|
| Exact symbol/string | `sg_keyword_search` |
| Concepts/semantic search | `sg_nls_search` |
| Trace usage/callers | `sg_find_references` |
| See implementation | `sg_go_to_definition` |
| Read full file | `sg_read_file` |
| Browse structure | `sg_list_files` |
| Find repos | `sg_list_repos` |
| Search commits | `sg_commit_search` |
| Track changes | `sg_diff_search` |
| Compare versions | `sg_compare_revisions` |

**Decision logic:**
1. Know the exact symbol? → `sg_keyword_search`
2. Know the concept, not the name? → `sg_nls_search`
3. Need definition of a symbol? → `sg_go_to_definition`
4. Need all callers/references? → `sg_find_references`
5. Need full file content? → `sg_read_file`

## Scoping (Always Do This)

```
repo:^github.com/ORG/REPO$           # Exact repo (preferred)
repo:github.com/ORG/                 # All repos in org
file:.*\.ts$                         # TypeScript only
file:src/api/                        # Specific directory
```

Start narrow. Expand only if results are empty.

## Efficiency Rules

- Chain searches logically: search → read → references → definition
- Don't re-search for the same pattern; use results from prior calls
- Prefer `sg_keyword_search` over `sg_nls_search` when you have exact terms
- Read 2-3 related files before synthesising, rather than one at a time
- Don't read 20+ remote files without writing code — once you understand the pattern, start implementing

## If Stuck

If MCP search returns no results:
1. Broaden the search query (synonyms, partial identifiers)
2. Try `sg_nls_search` for semantic matching
3. Use `sg_list_files` to browse the directory structure
4. Use `sg_list_repos` to verify the repository name

---

**Sourcegraph Repositories:** `github.com/sg-evals/kubernetes--v1.32.0`, `github.com/sg-evals/client-go--v0.32.0`, `github.com/sg-evals/api--v0.32.0`, `github.com/sg-evals/etcd-io-etcd`

# Kubernetes API Server Admission Webhook Chain

## Your Task

Find all Go source files in kubernetes/kubernetes that implement the API server admission webhook chain: the webhook admission controller, the webhook call dispatch, and the admission response aggregation.

## Context

You are working on a codebase task involving repos from the domain domain.

## Available Resources

The local `/workspace/` directory contains: sg-evals/kubernetes--v1.32.0, sg-evals/client-go--v0.32.0, sg-evals/api--v0.32.0, sg-evals/etcd-io-etcd.

**Note:** Additional repositories are accessible via Sourcegraph MCP tools:
- `sg-evals/etcd-io-etcd` (etcd-io/etcd)

```json

}
```

Include only the fields relevant to this task. Your answer is evaluated against a closed-world oracle — completeness matters.

1. MutatingAdmissionWebhook.Admit() / ValidatingAdmissionWebhook.Validate()
2. generic.Webhook.Dispatch()
3. dispatcher.Dispatch() with webhook iteration
4. Individual webhook calls (callAttrMutatingHook / callHook)
5. Response aggregation (patches for mutating, errors for validating)

**Detailed Narrative** explaining:
- How the generic webhook controller coordinates the admission process
- How mutating webhooks apply patches sequentially and track reinvocations
- How validating webhooks run in parallel and aggregate validation results
- How webhook configuration is dynamically loaded from Custom Resources
- How webhooks are filtered by namespace, object selectors, rules, and match conditions

The Dispatch() method iterates through applicable webhooks and calls callAttrMutatingHook() for each. It handles patch application, mutation tracking, reinvocation of webhooks when objects are mutated, and aggregates audit annotations.\\n   - staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/validating/dispatcher.go implements validatingDispatcher which dispatches admission requests to validating webhooks in parallel using goroutines. The Dispatch() method spawns concurrent webhook calls and aggregates validation errors. It collects all errors and returns the first one as a failure.\\n   - Both dispatchers inherit from the generic Dispatcher interface and use webhookutil.ClientManager for REST calls to webhook servers.\\n\\n4. **Admission Response Aggregation:**\\n   - staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/request/admissionreview.go provides CreateAdmissionObjects() to marshal admission requests and VerifyAdmissionResponse() to validate and extract response data. Its Admit() method invokes the generic webhook's Dispatch() method.\\n   - staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/validating/plugin.go implements the ValidatingAdmissionWebhook plugin that handles validating webhook admission. Its Validate() method invokes the generic webhook's Dispatch() method.\\n\\n3. **Webhook Call Dispatch (Webhook Invocation Chain):**\\n   - staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/mutating/dispatcher.go implements mutatingDispatcher which dispatches admission requests to mutating webhooks sequentially. The Dispatch() method iterates through applicable webhooks and calls callAttrMutatingHook() for each. It handles patch application, mutation tracking, reinvocation of webhooks when objects are mutated, and aggregates audit annotations.\\n   - staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/validating/dispatcher.go implements validatingDispatcher which dispatches admission requests to validating webhooks in parallel using goroutines. The Dispatch() method spawns concurrent webhook calls and aggregates validation errors. It collects all errors and returns the first one as a failure.\\n   - Both dispatchers inherit from the generic Dispatcher interface and use webhookutil.ClientManager for REST calls to webhook servers.\\n\\n4. **Admission Response Aggregation:**\\n   - staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/request/admissionreview.go provides CreateAdmissionObjects() to marshal admission requests and VerifyAdmissionResponse() to validate and extract response data. The VerifyAdmissionResponse() function aggregates response fields including patches, audit annotations, warnings, and rejection status.\\n   - staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/mutating/dispatcher.go aggregates patches from mutating webhooks using JSON patch operations and applies them sequentially to the object. It also aggregates audit annotations about mutations and failed-open scenarios.\\n   - staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/validating/dispatcher.go aggregates validation results by collecting errors from parallel webhook calls and returning the first error, while logging other errors.\\n\\n5. **Webhook Configuration Management:**\\n   - staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/configuration/configuration_manager.go provides the base polling mechanism for dynamically loading webhook configurations.\\n\\n6. **Webhook Filtering and Matching:**\\n   - staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/predicates/namespace/matcher.go implements namespace selector matching for exempting namespaces.\\n   - staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/predicates/object/matcher.go implements object label selector matching.\\n   - staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/predicates/rules/rules.go implements rule matching for verifying if webhook's registered rules match the request resource and operation.\\n   - staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/matchconditions/matcher.go implements CEL-based match condition evaluation.\\n\\n7. **Supporting Infrastructure:**\\n   - staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/accessors.go defines WebhookAccessor interface and implementations providing a unified view of mutating and validating webhooks.\\n   -
